# Welcome | Southside | Wiki

![Page cover](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252F3DrhIQHpghH4A9sQtkQ2%252FSouthside.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded8f76dc-4210-4014-bd84-e274af43c64b&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=381e5862&sv=2)

Welcome to **SouthSide RP**, a brand new experience built from the ground up! In this high-stakes server, you'll be indulged into a world where every decision could mean the difference between fortune and failure.

Whether you're a seasoned FiveM player or a new one, **SouthSide RP** provides an exhilarating environment where only the smartest and quickest survive.

Join now and see if you have what it takes to beat the clock and claim your fortune!

[](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/hub/socials)

![Cover](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FzRDoFpharcoNgjnOfEZn%252Fbackkground.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc849b132-fb87-418b-af6c-79db6604ce5c&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cda0dbca&sv=2)

# FAQ | Southside | Wiki

**How do I connect to the server?**

*   Search "SouthSide" in the server browser or press F8 `Connect`
    

**Where can I appeal my ban?**

*   You can appeal your ban via Discord and make a ticket.
    

**What are the controls for the city?**

*   You can find the controls [here](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/controls-commands)
    .
    

**How do I donate?**

*   You can find and donate to our store [here](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/hub/store)
    .
    

**What do I do if I am stuck under the map?**

*   If you are stuck under the map, please make a report in game with /report.
    

**What if my steam account isn't found?**

*   Please make a support ticket within the discord.
    

[PreviousConnectionchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/connection)
[NextControls/Commandschevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/controls-commands)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Voice Output | Southside | Wiki

1.  Press the ESC button on your keyboard to open the GTA home screen
    
2.  Select the `Settings` button at the top
    
3.  Select the `Voice Chat` button on the side panel
    
4.  Check the `Voice Chat Enabled` is set to `On`
    
5.  Check the `Output Device` matches the device you are using to listen to audio
    
6.  Check the `Voice Chat Volume` slider is to the right
    
7.  Check the `Microphone Enabled` is set to `On`
    
8.  Check the `Input Device` matches the device you are using to speak through
    
9.  Check the `Microphone Volume` slider is to the right
    
10.  If using `Voice Activated` check the `Microphone Sensitivity` slider is to the right
    
11.  If using `Push To Talk` use the **N** key to speak in game, you can be rebind in the settings also
    

[PreviousRP Termschevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/rp-terms)
[NextInventory Systemchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/inventory-system)

# Character Creation | Southside | Wiki

Once you load into the server for the first time, you'll be brought here to this landing page to create your character for the very first time!

When you're ready, make sure to put a First and Last name, and no they don't have to be literal names.

Fill out the information below, and continue on to the next screen.

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FMG0dvgV29HHYaw1QFLgx%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_221616.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c67256a-0f3c-4714-a9e3-68eff6c95c21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da4cb0ee&sv=2)

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FZVAWtNRhTVyGAS8LSDHR%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_221652.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D749ee574-febc-4760-bf65-8d4248f0dea7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d8e0ec2&sv=2)

After you press **Confirm,** you are now ready to create your character!

Make sure to take your time here, you can always get re-skinned if you have any issues during this.

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252Fvk942BBbVqbgL370XY46%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_222050.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decfd9809-deae-49c6-a112-27981a55c343&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf5eef1&sv=2)

Once you are done, press "Save Changes" and you will be ready to explore the city of Los Santos. If you have any issues during character creation, please make a report in-game.

[PreviousInventory Systemchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/inventory-system)
[NextGeneral Knowledgechevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge)

# RP Terms | Southside | Wiki

PHRASE

MEANING

**Fly Out, Fly In**

`You will be leaving the city or coming in to the city`

**City**

`Server`

**Head Pop**

`Game Crashed`

**Email**

`Referring to Discord`

**In My Head**

`AFK`

**Tsunami, Storm**

`Server Restart`

**Locals**

`AI/NPC’s in the city`

**Flex Muscle**

`Press a key`

**Eyes**

`Your screen`

**Headache**

`Experiencing frame drops, Lagging, etc`

**Spider**

`You are glitching, pressing spacebar should fix it`

**Wizard**

`There is a hacker/modder terrorizing the city`

**The Boat/Clean the Boat**

`Community Service for rule breaks`

**City Tow**

`Car Wipe`

**Scuffed**

`FiveM is acting up, your game is messed up`

**Pockets**

`Your inventory`

**Brain**

`Your PC`

**Look Through your Eyes**

`Press “V” to go in 1st person view mode`

**Voice Box**

`Microphone, mic settings, etc`

**Purple Eyes**

`They are Livestreaming`

**Angels**

`Referring to Staff`

# Connection | Southside | Wiki

If you'd like to know how you can start playing follow the instructions below.

⬇️ Download & Install Grand Theft Auto V

⬇️ Download and install "[FiveMarrow-up-right](https://fivem.net/)
"

🔍Search "SouthSide" in the server browser and press connect

✅Make sure to join the discord & verify within the discord channel. F8 `Connect-COMING-SOON`

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FnXakK7N5OLxJxcbiSZ5o%252FVeri.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D844eb803-b523-4057-97a8-776e7ff7b6e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d6b00b6&sv=2)

You should be able to join the server and connect. If you have any questions or issues, please make a ticket within the discord.

# Controls/Commands | Southside | Wiki

circle-info

Looking for something in particular? Use the search bar at the top right of your screen on the gitbook.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/controls-commands#keybinds-within-the-server)

KeyBinds within the server


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Action

T

To use the chat

E

Interaction

N

Push to Talk ( Default)

ESC

Brings up the esc menu

F2

Inventory

L

Show Chat/Active/Close

Enter

Answer Call

M

Open Phone

F5

Open Tablet ( if you have one)

TAB

Inventory Hotbar

R

Reload Weapon

1-5

Use Hotbar Item

F1

Radial Menu

L ALT

(Alt Look)

CAPS

Talk over Radio

F10

Scoreboard

H

Hands Up

X

Cancel Emote

F5

Emote Menu

B

Point

E

Interact

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/controls-commands#vehicle)

Vehicle


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Action

K

Open vehicle Menu (in vehicle)

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/controls-commands#server-commands)

Server Commands


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Command

Action

/job

Shows current Job

/jailtime

Check your jail time

/druglb

Shows you the drug leaderboard

/dice

Rolls dice

/gang

Check your Gang

/repair

Repair your vehicle

/emotemenu

Opens the emote menu

/reloadskin

Reloads your character

/block

Blocks a player from sending you PMs

/unblock

Unblocks a player from sending you PM's

/PM

Sends a private msg to a player

/postal

Sets a waypoint to a postal area on the map.

/clear

Clears chat for yourself

# Inventory System | Southside | Wiki

Here is what the base inventory looks like

1-5 are for slots to hold important items called "Quick Slots"

You can also place items on the ground.

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FRpp5O6iPZ2SgMibtFILO%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_220930.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3cb962b-61c4-466b-920c-e8b7b3debd2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=daf010c4&sv=2)

When you right click an item, the following shows.

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FuwgxsKzOkmoeSD3c3UrG%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_224402.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e9a3b0c-9fcf-439d-aac3-3ad7c83e848e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=440314c1&sv=2)

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FI5MiUDK0rDjc0vNPENLz%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_224421.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82bd967b-9411-4e92-b4c7-08575dae4abc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37c23bf1&sv=2)

At the top of the Inventory, you can either press "Q" or "E" to switch from inventory to Utilities.

The right body image shows injuries to your body, so if you hover over the part, it will say if the limb is injured.

You also have 3 slots, one for **backpack or duffle bag, wallet to hold IDs and your phone.**

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FCWvaCrX1wTV2StDLM5V4%252FScreenshot_2026-01-29_223943.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8a67a9d-6a02-49bc-be43-6fc0220db394&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6dd8613&sv=2)

Top Right of your screen has your server id, in-game time, if your mic is on or off, and job.

# Combat Logging | Southside | Wiki

**You are not allowed to intentionally close the game to avoid interactions or an unwanted outcome.** This includes disconnecting, force-quitting, or otherwise leaving the server to escape roleplay situations, consequences, or interactions with other players.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/combat_logging#what-constitutes-combat-logging)

What Constitutes Combat Logging

*   **Intentional Disconnects:** Leaving the game (using F8, Alt+F4, or any other method) during an active roleplay scenario to avoid arrest, robbery, death, or any other consequence.
    
*   **Unreported Crashes:** Failing to report a legitimate game crash that occurs during a scene. If your game crashes, you must immediately notify staff or provide proof if requested.
    
*   **Internet Manipulation:** Deliberately disconnecting your internet or causing a network failure to escape a roleplay situation.
    
*   **Avoiding Roleplay:** Leaving the server to avoid any form of roleplay, including police interactions, robberies, or ongoing scenes.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/combat_logging#examples-of-combat-logging)

Examples of Combat Logging

*   **F8’ing during a police scene** to avoid arrest or questioning.
    
*   **F8’ing to avoid getting robbed** or losing your items.
    
*   **F8’ing to avoid any RP** that you do not want to participate in.
    
*   **Pulling out your internet cord** or otherwise disconnecting your internet to escape a situation.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/combat_logging#additional)

Additional

*   **Reporting Crashes:** If your game crashes mid-scene, you must report it to staff or the involved parties as soon as possible. Be prepared to provide proof (such as a screenshot or video) if requested.
    
*   **AFK Protocol:** If you need to go AFK, you must go to a green zone (safe zone) first. Do not leave your character unattended in active roleplay areas.
    
*   **Rejoin When Possible:** If disconnected unintentionally, rejoin the server and resume the roleplay as soon as possible.
    

[PreviousFail RPchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/fail_rp)
[NextRobbing , Scamming , Kidnappingchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming)

# New Life Rule | Southside | Wiki

**When a player is killed for any reason, you are prohibited from remembering any previous events that led up to your current state. You may not return to the location where you died for a 15-minute period.**

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#what-the-new-life-rule-means)

What the New Life Rule Means

**Memory Loss:** After death, your character forgets all details, events, and people involved in the situation that led to your death. You cannot seek revenge, share information, or act on anything related to your previous life.

**No Return:** You are not allowed to return to the location of your death for at least 15 minutes, even if the scenario is ongoing or your friends are still involved.

**No Revenge:** You may not use any information from the events that led to your death to retaliate, inform others, or influence future roleplay.

**Double Tap Rule:** If you are "double tapped" (someone stands over you and shoots you in the head twice), you forget everything leading up to your death, even if EMS revives you.

**Flat-Backed :** If you are flat-backed you can't remember the last 15 minutes of RP, even if EMS revives you.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#examples-of-new-life-rule)

Examples of New Life Rule:

*   **Returning to the Scene:** Going back to the place where you died before the 15-minute timer is up.
    
*   **Remembering Events:** Using knowledge from before your death to influence your actions, such as identifying or seeking out your killers.
    
*   **Revenge Kill:** Tracking down and attacking those responsible for your previous death.
    
*   **Double Tap Scenario:** If you are executed (double tapped), you cannot remember anything from the incident, regardless of EMS revival.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#additional)

Additional

*   **EMS Revive:** If you are revived by EMS and were not double tapped, you may roleplay minor memory loss or confusion, but you still cannot remember specific details or identities from the events that led to your death.
    
*   **Communication:** Do not relay information from your previous life to other players, in or out of character.
    
*   **Roleplay Integrity:** Respect the New Life Rule to ensure fair and immersive roleplay for everyone on the server.
    

[PreviousMetagamingchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming)
[NextValue Lifechevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/value-life)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [What the New Life Rule Means](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#what-the-new-life-rule-means)
    
*   [Examples of New Life Rule:](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#examples-of-new-life-rule)
    
*   [Additional](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife#additional)

# Value Life | Southside | Wiki

You must always roleplay fear for your character’s life when faced with threats of serious harm or death. This means acting realistically in dangerous situations, such as when someone has a weapon pointed at you or you are outnumbered.

Do not act recklessly or unrealistically when your character’s life is clearly at risk. For example, do not attempt to fight back or run if you are surrounded and unarmed, or if compliance is the only reasonable option.

If you are being held at gunpoint, taken hostage, or otherwise placed in a life-threatening scenario, your character must prioritize survival and act accordingly (e.g., comply with demands, avoid escalating the situation).

Bystanders and civilians must also show realistic fear for their lives during violent or criminal events, attempting to flee or avoid danger rather than intervening unless escape is impossible.

Do not use out-of-character knowledge or game mechanics to escape life-threatening situations unrealistically (e.g., combat logging, exploiting safe zones, or respawning to avoid consequences).

Breaking FearRP or failing to value your character’s life may result in disciplinary action, including warnings, temporary bans, or permanent bans depending on the severity of the offense. **In a 1v1 Situation you must fear for your life if your gun is not pulled out.**

**Examples of Rule Breaches**

*   Charging armed individuals without a weapon or backup.
    
*   Refusing to comply with armed robbers’ demands when you are at a clear disadvantage.
    
*   Returning to a scene of your own death (violates New Life Rule as well).
    
*   Using OOC (out-of-character) chat or disconnecting to avoid roleplay consequences.
    

[PreviousNew Life Rulechevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife)
[NextFail RPchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/fail_rp)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Power gaming | Southside | Wiki

**Power gaming refers to behaviors that unfairly benefit your character or disturb the roleplaying experience by imposing outcomes or neglecting realistic repercussions.** This includes forcing actions on others without giving them a chance to respond, exploiting game mechanics, or avoiding consequences in unrealistic ways.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/powergaming#what-constitutes-power-gaming)

What Constitutes Power Gaming

*   **Forcing Outcomes:** Forcing actions or decisions on other players without allowing them a fair chance to react or respond through roleplay.
    
*   **Ignoring Realism:** Taking actions that your character could not realistically perform, or neglecting logical consequences for your actions.
    
*   **Exploiting Mechanics:** Using game mechanics, glitches, or exploits to gain an unfair advantage or to escape a roleplay scenario.
    
*   **Mini Modding (OOC): Must remain in character at all times.**
    
*   **Clothing Store:** You CANNOT rob someone that is in a clothing menu in the clothing store.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/powergaming#examples-of-power-gaming)

Examples of Power Gaming

*   **Running Into Green Zones (GZ):** You cannot run into a green zone (safe zone) during a gunfight, robbery, or any active scene to avoid roleplay or consequences.
    
*   **Teleport Abuse:** Running into a teleport location, such as the car dealership or other scripted teleports, to escape from a scene or evade other players.
    
*   **Initiating in Bulletproof Vehicles:** Attempting to start or escalate a hostile situation while inside a bulletproof or otherwise unrealistic vehicle.
    
*   **Exploiting:** Using any kind of exploit, glitch, or unintended game mechanic to gain an advantage (e.g., bug abuse, item duplication).
    
*   **Emote Cancelling:** Cancelling emotes to avoid being restrained, injured, or to gain an unfair advantage in combat.
    
*   **TMF Roll & Spamming X:** Using TMF Roll, spamming the "X" key while shooting, or any similar actions to dodge bullets or gain an unrealistic edge in combat.
    
*   **Avoiding RP in GZ:** Running into a green zone or safe area specifically to avoid ongoing roleplay or the consequences of your actions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/powergaming#additional)

Additional

*   **Fair Play:** Always give other players a chance to roleplay and respond to your actions. Avoid actions that remove their ability to participate in the scene.
    
*   **No Exploiting:** Any form of exploiting, glitching, or abusing scripts is strictly forbidden and will be treated as a serious offense.
    

[PreviousFemale Harassmentchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge/female)
[NextMetagamingchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming)

# Interrupting / Injecting into RP | Southside | Wiki

**Roleplay injection** (also known as **interrupting RP**) occurs when a player forcefully inserts themselves into an active roleplay scenario without proper in-character reasoning, buildup, or relevance to the ongoing situation.

Players must **not interfere** with active roleplay unless their character has a **clear, logical, and realistic reason** to be involved. What does this look like?

*   You cannot inject yourself into active roleplay scenes, 3rd party an active gunfight or police chase. Police can inject themselves into any type of criminal roleplay being committed as it is their duty.
    
*   You are passing by a shootout and see one person left that's apart of a shootout you're not involved in. You and your friends decide to hop out while he's healing and attempt to rob him. The player MUST make sure you are aware that they're involved in an active scene and once that is announce you must leave immediately.
    
*   Police are chasing a player you have beef with so you hop out of your vehicle and shoot their tires to lower the odds of them escaping. You're injecting into the chase that has nothing to do with you and you will be punished for griefing/injecting.
    
*   If a certain group is doing a heist with police on scene another group cannot attempt to counter the active scene.
    

[PreviousLow Effort RPchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/low-effort-rp)
[NextWill & Testamentchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament)

# Female Harassment | Southside | Wiki

**General**

*   All players must treat each other with respect and courtesy. Harassment, discrimination, and offensive behavior-including sexism and gender-based hate speech-will not be tolerated under any circumstances.
    
*   The server is a safe and inclusive environment for everyone, regardless of gender. Any attempt to make others uncomfortable or unsafe will be met with disciplinary action.
    

**Prohibited Behaviors**

*   Any form of harassment, including but not limited to sexist comments, unwanted sexual advances, threats, doxing, or cyberstalking, is strictly forbidden.
    
*   Use of gender-based slurs, derogatory language, or offensive jokes targeting women will result in immediate consequences, up to and including permanent bans.
    
*   Unwanted sexual or romantic messages, in-game or via direct messages, are not allowed.
    
*   Non-consensual sexual roleplay or any form of sexual harassment is strictly prohibited and will result in a permanent ban.
    
*   Repeatedly targeting, griefing, or trolling female players, either in-character or out-of-character, is considered harassment and will not be tolerated.
    

**Consent and Roleplay Boundaries**

*   All NSFW or erotic roleplay must be consensual and agreed upon by all involved parties. Non-consensual acts or harassment of any kind are strictly forbidden.
    
*   If a player indicates discomfort or asks for a specific behavior to stop (either in-character or OOC), you must immediately cease that behavior. Failure to do so will result in disciplinary action.
    
*   Any form of sexual roleplay, including implied or explicit acts, must be conducted only with prior consent and in appropriate, private channels if permitted by server rules.
    

**Reporting and Enforcement**

*   Players are encouraged to report any incidents of harassment or inappropriate behavior to server staff or moderators immediately.
    
*   Attempts to find loopholes or skirt around these rules will be treated as violations and may result in punishment at the discretion of the staff.
    
*   All reports of harassment will be taken seriously and investigated thoroughly. Disciplinary actions may include warnings, temporary suspensions, or permanent bans depending on the severity of the offense.
    

[PreviousPlayer Reports Policychevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge/player-reports-policy)
[NextPower gamingchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/powergaming)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Fail RP | Southside | Wiki

**You are not allowed to engage in any roleplay that is unrealistic to a FiveM RP setting.** All actions must be believable and grounded in the context of the server’s world.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/fail_rp#what-constitutes-fail-rp)

What Constitutes Fail RP

*   **Unrealistic Actions:** Performing actions that would not be possible or believable in real life or within the game’s roleplay environment.
    
*   **Ignoring Roleplay Consequences:** Failing to react appropriately to dangerous or life-threatening situations.
    
*   **Breaking Immersion:** Doing things that disrupt the roleplay experience for others or break the immersion of the scenario.
    
*   Scenes do not continue after tsunami unless both parties agree to carry on the scene. (Unless it is involving pd where you have to continue after tsunami)
    
*   If someone is on a crutch you SHOULD NOT be intentionally trying to kill them. If you are on a crutch you should try your best to get away from the shooting taking place, you should not be trying to get in the middle of the shootout. This would fall under failing to fear.
    
*   Male players cannot use a female ped to have a smaller hitbox.
    
*   If carrying a large weapon you must roleplay realistically with a corresponding bag.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/fail_rp#examples-of-fail-rp)

Examples of Fail RP

*   **Ignoring Threats:** Not putting your hands up or failing to comply when you have guns pointed at you.
    
*   **Talking While Dead:** Communicating after your character has died, especially if you have been “double tapped” (a player stands over you and shoots you in the head twice).
    
*   **Unrealistic Vehicle Use:** Carrying 3-4 friends stacked on a single motorcycle.
    
*   **Exploiting Emotes:** Using emotes to glitch through walls or into secured areas that should not be accessible.
    
*   **Unrealistic Escapes:** Performing stunts or maneuvers that are not possible for your character or vehicle, such as jumping from extreme heights and surviving without injury.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/fail_rp#additional)

Additional

*   **Stay in Character:** Always act as your character would in real life, given the circumstances.
    
*   **Respect the Scene:** Do not do anything that would break the immersion or realism of the ongoing roleplay.
    
*   **No Exploiting:** Do not use glitches, bugs, or exploits to perform actions that would otherwise be impossible.
    

[PreviousValue Lifechevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/value-life)
[NextCombat Loggingchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/combat_logging)

# Player Reports Policy | Southside | Wiki

_This policy is to outline basic reporting etiquette and standards when reporting an individual, or a gang enterprise._

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge/player-reports-policy#report-submissions)

**Report Submissions:**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reports can be made in-city, as well as creating a ticket within the SSRP Discord Server. Every report made must have evidence to support the claim being made. **Clips must be 1-2 minute long and include audio**. Failing to do so will render the report **invalid** until further evidence is provided. **Clips must be reported within 24 hours or they will be deemed invalid**.

If you are rule breaking within your clip, trying to report another party, your clip then becomes invalid. **No Revenge Reporting.** Only submit reports for violations specified on this page. Submitting tickets for non-rule breaks or things you believe are rule breaks will result in an immediate denial of your report and it will be closed instantly. **In-city Reporting:** /report _(report command in-city)_ **Discord Reporting: #**support-tickets **Ban Appeals:** You can create a ticket within the #support-tickets section in the discord. If you have clip watch role, and you get 2-3 + kills you need to clip the whole fight.

**Note:** If a gang member is banned for cheating, the gang will receive 2 strikes. The player in question is also required to purchase a cheater unban, and must factory reset (with proof). Cheaters will also get a 'MUST STREAM' role in SSRP and must clip with approved software for **all gameplay sessions.** Players who get banned twice for cheating will be **blacklisted from the server.**

# Low Effort RP | Southside | Wiki

**Low Effort Roleplay** is defined as skipping meaningful roleplay, improvisation, or character development in order to quickly reach an outcome. Roleplay is about storytelling, interaction, and immersion—**not rushing scenes or forcing results**.

All roleplay scenarios must be given adequate time to develop, and all involved players should clearly understand the in-character reasoning behind actions and events.

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/low-effort-rp#what-constitutes-low-effort-rp)

What Constitutes Low Effort RP

*   Rushing or skipping dialogue to immediately escalate a situation
    
*   Ignoring logical buildup, context, or character motivation
    
*   Forcing outcomes without allowing other players to respond or contribute
    
*   Performing actions without explaining intent or reasoning through RP
    
*   Treating RP scenarios as tasks to complete rather than scenes to develop
    
*   You are not allowed to **intentionally** camp someone.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/low-effort-rp#examples-of-low-effort-rp)

Examples of Low Effort RP

*   Immediately pulling a weapon or initiating violence with no verbal RP or buildup
    
*   Kidnapping, robbing, or killing a character without interaction or justification
    
*   Speed-running negotiations, interrogations, or medical RP
    
*   Using one-line or repetitive responses to avoid meaningful interaction
    
*   Ignoring reactions, injuries, or consequences to push a scene forward
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/low-effort-rp#additional-guidelines)

Additional Guidelines

*   **Develop the Scene:** Allow interactions to flow naturally and give others time to respond.
    
*   **Stay Immersed:** Your character’s actions should align with their background, emotions, and situation.
    
*   **Communicate Clearly:** Ensure other players understand why your character is acting the way they are through RP.
    
*   **Quality Over Speed:** Outcomes should be earned through roleplay, not rushed.
    

[PreviousRules of Engagementchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement)
[NextInterrupting / Injecting into RPchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/interrupting-injecting-into-rp)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Rules of Engagement | Southside | Wiki

**Initiation is the act of making your hostile intentions clear before taking aggressive or criminal actions against another player.**

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#initiation-guidelines)

Initiation Guidelines

*   Civilians should **NOT** be targeted by gang members unless the civilian initiates the interaction.
    
    *   This includes
        
        *   Civilian Players that do no crime.
            
        *   Criminals - Players that are not in a gang, but engage in criminal activity.
            
        *   Gang Members - Criminal Involved in a gang.
            
        
    
*   **Verbal or Physical Cues:** Initiation can be done through clear verbal threats, commands, or obvious physical actions (such as aiming a weapon).
    
*   **No Silent Aggression:** Do not attack, rob, or steal from another player without proper initiation. Surprise attacks without clear intent are considered Fail RP.
    
*   **Time to React:** Always give the other player reasonable time to react or comply after initiating.
    
*   **Holding/Dumping Bodies:** Players cannot hold or dump bodies so that EMS cannot find them.
    
*   **If you are an Unofficial faction, your sliding limit is 3.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#examples-of-initiation)

Examples of Initiation

*   **Aiming is Initiation:** Pointing a weapon at someone is considered initiation and signals your hostile intent.
    
*   **Robbing Trunks:** Attempting to rob the trunk of someone’s vehicle is an act of initiation.
    
*   **Taking or Driving Away with Someone Else’s Car:** Entering, stealing, or driving away in another player’s vehicle is considered initiation and may lead to further hostile actions.
    
*   **Verbal Threats:** Clearly stating your demands or intentions (e.g., “Put your hands up or I’ll shoot!”) is a valid form of initiation.
    
*   **Examples of Civlian - Gang Interaction**
    
    *   A gang member is in the coke lab with 3 other gang members & they interact with another player farming coke, leading to a robbery. This situation is OKAY because farming drugs is a criminal activity.
        
    *   A civilian is putting gas in their car next to a group of gang members. The gang members interact with the civilian, leading to a robbery. This situation is NOT okay because the civilian is not provoking them leading up to being robbed.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#additional)

Additional

*   **No Random Attacks:** Do not initiate hostile actions without a valid reason or roleplay context.
    
*   **No Ambushes Without Initiation:** Even in ambushes, you must make your intentions clear before engaging.
    
*   **Respect Cooldowns:** Do not repeatedly initiate on the same player or group without proper roleplay development or cooldowns.
    

[PreviousRobbing , Scamming , Kidnappingchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming)
[NextLow Effort RPchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/low-effort-rp)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Initiation Guidelines](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#initiation-guidelines)
    
*   [Examples of Initiation](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#examples-of-initiation)
    
*   [Additional](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement#additional)

# Robbing , Scamming , Kidnapping | Southside | Wiki

Robbing **Definition:** Taking property from another person by using force, violence, intimidation, or the threat of force, with the intent to deprive the victim of that property.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#robbing-rules)

Robbing Rules

*   **No Killing After Robbery:** You may not kill someone after robbing them. The purpose of robbery is theft, not murder. **Example:** You rob someone and they comply and walk away — you cannot shoot them afterward. **Exception:** If the victim becomes an immediate threat during the robbery (pulls a gun, attacks, or runs after clear commands), lethal force may be justified.
    
*   Robberies must **ONLY** take place at night.
    
*   **No Robbing During Shootouts:** You may not start or continue a robbery during an active shootout or gunfight. If a shootout begins, the robbery is considered cancelled.
    
*   **Protected Roles:** You may not rob EMS, lawyers, judges, or on-duty police at any time.
    
*   **No Chain Robbing:** You must wait 2 hours before robbing the same player again. Repeatedly robbing multiple players back-to-back may be treated as harassment or **Powergaming.** **Example:** You rob Player A at 6:00 PM — you cannot rob Player A again until 8:00 PM. Robbing Player B shortly after is allowed, but going on a nonstop robbery spree is not.
    
*   **Compliance & Threat Clarification:** A player is considered compliant if they follow clear verbal commands and do not attempt to flee, fight, or alert others. Non-compliance during the robbery may escalate the situation, but killing after the robbery is finished is not allowed. **Example:** _If the victim listens, gives items, and leaves, the situation is over. You cannot chase and kill them afterward._
    
*   **Business Employees:** You may not rob on-duty employees at businesses. Employees must be wearing business attire to be protected; if someone is wearing gang attire while clocked in, they can be robbed.
    
*   **Robbery Ratio:** All robbing encounters must be a 3-to-1 ratio (robbers to victim). You cannot rob someone if you do not have at least three robbers present. All robbers must have a weapon.
    
*   **No Forced Withdrawals:** You cannot make someone pull money from their bank account or use in-game banking features during a robbery.
    
*   **Robbing PD:** You may not rob police officers for any police-issued equipment under any circumstance. This includes weapons, tasers, radios, body armor, health kits, or any item clearly provided by the Police Department. You may only rob officers who are clearly off duty and not acting in any law enforcement capacity. The interaction must still follow standard robbery RP rules and remain realistic. **Example:** _**An off-duty officer at a bar or out of uniform may be treated as a civilian if there is valid RP.**_ **On-Duty Officer Robbery (Very Limited Exception):** Robbing an on-duty officer is only allowed if there is strong, ongoing RP backstory or direct reasoning tied to the situation. This is meant for long-term storylines, not random encounters. **Example:** _**You have an established gang storyline where an officer previously seized your illegal weapon, and you confront them later specifically to retrieve that weapon.**_ If you rob an on-duty officer during valid RP, you may only take illegal items or items that directly belong to your character’s storyline (e.g., a confiscated illegal weapon). You may not take any standard police-issued gear. Being arrested or raided does not give you the right to target multiple officers to “get your stuff back.” You may not organize or participate in mass robberies against police as retaliation. If you are unsure whether an item is police-issued, do not take it. When in doubt, leave it. Claiming ignorance after taking obvious duty equipment will not be tolerated.
    
    This exception exists strictly for players with deep, ongoing RP storylines involving specific officers. It is not intended for random robberies, quick revenge scenarios, or loot-focused gameplay. The RP must be meaningful and justifiable. Any attempt to exploit this rule for easy gear, revenge, or low-effort robberies will result in staff action. Continued abuse will lead to this exception being removed entirely, making all officer robberies disallowed regardless of RP context. **PD is only robbable of illegal contraband!** **DO NOT TAKE: Med Kits, Ammo, PD items/weapons, or donuts. You cannot steal PD vehicles either. Robbable items include:**
    
    *   **Contraband that was taken off you.**
        
    *   **Illegal guns**
        
    *   **Gun store guns**
        
    *   **Drugs**
        
    *   **Blueprints**
        
    *   **Dirty and clean cash**
        
    *   **Bank items (drills, drill bits, thermite)**
        
    *   **Raw materials.**
        
    

**PD are not loot bags, they are the main RP of the city and this rule is in place to keep them in city and able to do their job. With more PD comes better roleplay and more chances to hit banks!**

*   **Robbing EMS: YOU CANNOT ROB EMS OR STEAL THEIR CARS. Also, CANNOT kill them.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#examples-of-robbing)

Examples of Robbing

*   Pulling up with three people after a bank robbery to rob someone of their belongings.
    
*   Forcing someone to hand over their items or cash by threatening them with weapons.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#scamming)

Scamming

**Scamming Definition:** Scamming is the act of deceiving someone in order to gain money or an advantage.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#scamming-rules)

Scamming Rules

*   **Scam Limit:** You are not allowed to scam players for more than $50,000 in in-game cash per incident.
    
*   **No Item Scams Above Limit:** If you scam someone for an item or service, the value cannot exceed $50,000.
    
*   **No OOC Scams:** All scams must be in-character and roleplayed. Out-of-character (OOC) scamming is strictly prohibited.
    
*   **Loot Boxing:** Robbing cops or individuals without valid reasons, solely for personal gain, is not permitted. This includes pocketing wiping someone without justification.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#examples-of-scamming)

Examples of Scamming

*   Selling a black market item or weapon for $50,000 and not giving the item to the buyer.
    
*   Promising a service or product and intentionally failing to deliver after receiving payment.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/robbing_scamming#kidnapping)

Kidnapping

**Kidnapping** is a high-risk roleplay scenario and must be treated seriously, realistically, and with proper roleplay buildup. All kidnapping scenarios must involve clear intent, meaningful interaction, and fair opportunities for all parties involved.

Kidnapping should **never be rushed**, forced, or used as a shortcut to achieve an outcome. If you kidnap someone for a hostage situation you may only hold them hostage for 15 minutes.

You cannot kidnap on Duty **EMS, PD, or workers who are clocked in**. (If you have a hostage and by the time you get to the place you wanted to rob someone is already robbing it you must let the hostage go after 15 minutes.)

You cannot use a **fake hostage.** All hostages must be acquired through roleplay and the hostage cannot be in on it. (Cannot be your friend, gang/group member, or someone that agreed to being a hostage for a percentage of the pay.)

[PreviousCombat Loggingchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/combat_logging)
[NextRules of Engagementchevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/rules-of-engagement)

# Will & Testament | Southside | Wiki

A **will** may be created to determine the distribution of certain assets in the event of your character’s **permanent death**. Wills exist to support long-term roleplay and character legacy and must follow all server restrictions listed below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament#general-rules)

General Rules

*   A will **must be submitted and approved by a judge PRIOR to your character’s death**.
    
*   Wills submitted after death will **not** be honored.
    
*   Once approved, the will becomes **binding** upon character death.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament#what-can-be-willed)

What Can Be Willed

Only the following assets may be included in a will:

*   **Money** (maximum of **$500,000**)
    
*   **Vehicles** (maximum of 2)
    
*   **Properties (Limited to 1)**
    

❌ **Inventory items of any kind may NOT be willed.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament#distribution-restrictions)

Distribution Restrictions

*   All willed assets (**money, vehicles, and properties**) must be left to **one single individual**.
    
*   That individual acts as the **executor** and may decide what to do with the inherited assets (keep, sell, transfer, etc.).
    
*   Assets **cannot** be split between multiple people.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament#housing-and-ownership-limits)

Housing & Ownership Limits

*   The **housing cap still applies** to inherited properties.
    
*   If a property is willed to someone who is already at their housing cap:
    
    *   The property will enter **default status**
        
    *   The property will be **reclaimed by the city**
        
    
*   Vehicles and properties inherited still count toward the recipient’s allowed maximums.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/will-and-testament#prohibited-actions)

Prohibited Actions

*   Creating or modifying a will **after** death or while facing imminent death
    
*   Using wills to bypass asset caps, inventory rules, or server economy limits
    
*   Transferring assets outside of the approved will process
    

[PreviousInterrupting / Injecting into RPchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/interrupting-injecting-into-rp)
[NextZoneschevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones)

Last updated 3 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Metagaming | Southside | Wiki

**Metagaming is considered as using outside information to gain in-game knowledge for your advantage.** This undermines fair play and realism in roleplay and is strictly prohibited.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#what-constitutes-metagaming)

What Constitutes Metagaming

**Stream Sniping:** You cannot watch or listen to any live streams (Discord, YouTube, Twitch, etc.) that may provide you with in-game information while you are actively playing. Using someone’s live stream to find their location to interact in any way is considered metagaming and is punishable as such.

**Out-of-Character Knowledge:** You may not use any information your character would not realistically know, including details learned from OOC chat, forums, streams, or other players outside of the game, to influence your in-game actions. **Voice Metagaming:** You cannot voice ID an individual when wearing a mask. **Discord**: There will be no use of Discord while being in-game.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#examples-of-metagaming)

Examples of Metagaming

*   **Watching a friend’s stream to find out where other players are or what they are doing, then using that information in your own gameplay.**
    
*   **Receiving or giving tips, warnings, or updates about in-game events through text messages, phone calls, or any means outside of the game’s built-in communication systems.**
    
*   **Identifying a voice in RP after you were robbed so that you could get your get-back even though you don't know them in RP.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#additional)

Additional

*   **Stay In-Character:** All communication and decision-making should be based solely on what your character knows and experiences in-game.
    
*   **No Ghosting:** Do not use information from spectating, streams, or other outside sources to influence your gameplay.
    
*   **Report Metagaming:** If you suspect metagaming, report it to server staff with evidence. Do not take matters into your own hands.
    

[PreviousPower gamingchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/powergaming)
[NextNew Life Rulechevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/valuinglife)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [What Constitutes Metagaming](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#what-constitutes-metagaming)
    
*   [Examples of Metagaming](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#examples-of-metagaming)
    
*   [Additional](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/metagaming#additional)

# Greenzone | Southside | Wiki

**Greenzones are designated safe zones where no crime or hostile actions are allowed.** These areas are intended to provide a safe, conflict-free environment for all players. Greenzones include : EMS

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#greenzone-guidelines)

Greenzone Guidelines

*   **No Killing:** You may not kill or attempt to kill anyone within a Greenzone.
    
*   **No Escaping Conflict:** You may not drive or run into a Greenzone to escape or prevent conflict from a previous or ongoing scene.
    
*   **No Scamming:** Scamming or deceiving other players for money, items, or information is strictly prohibited within Greenzones.
    
*   **No Vehicle Theft:** You may not steal, attempt to steal, or tamper with vehicles within a Greenzone.
    
*   **No Chain Abuse:** Do not repeatedly enter and exit a Greenzone (e.g., running out to shoot someone and then running back in for safety).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#examples-of-greenzone-violations)

Examples of Greenzone Violations

*   **Going back and forth:** Running out of the Greenzone to shoot someone, then running back in to avoid retaliation.
    
*   **Starting a robbery or fight:** Attempting to rob, attack, or intimidate someone within a Greenzone.
    
*   **Escaping into a Greenzone:** Entering a Greenzone to avoid being caught, robbed, or harmed after a hostile encounter elsewhere.
    
*   **Scamming or stealing:** Attempting to scam or steal from someone while both parties are inside a Greenzone.
    
*   If that player does not leave after a gz after the 10 minute timer you can engage with them.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#additional)

Additional

*   **Roleplay Respect:** Treat Greenzones as real-life safe spaces (e.g., police stations, hospitals, government buildings, staff ran events or other designated areas).
    
*   **No Loopholes:** Do not attempt to exploit Greenzone rules for personal gain or to avoid consequences.
    
*   **Staff Discretion:** Staff may take action for any behavior in Greenzones that disrupts the intended safe environment.
    
*   Gangs are allowed to give other enemy gang members that are in a greenzone 10 minutes to leave the respective greenzone. If they don’t leave the greenzone within that 10 minutes you are able to report them for power gaming/low effort role play. Both parties still need to initiate on one another properly with proper reasoning and roleplay.
    
*   Greenzones are valid for a span of 10 minutes until it is considered NITRP, they are meant to be a criminal activity free zone however staying in one without being in a scene or clocked in will result in a punishment.
    

[PreviousZoneschevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones)
[NextFaction Ruleschevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/faction_rules)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Greenzone Guidelines](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#greenzone-guidelines)
    
*   [Examples of Greenzone Violations](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#examples-of-greenzone-violations)
    
*   [Additional](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/zones/greenzone#additional)

# General Knowledge | Southside | Wiki

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#introduction)

Introduction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the introduction to our server rules, which will display many sections of our server rules that break down our TOS guidelines, general RP rules and conduct, turf guidelines, and gang conduct.

Our goal is to provide you with the best experiences on our RP server and give you a general outline of our standards within our server. Remember, everyone is obligated to follow the same rule sets and is expected to know the rules upon joining our server.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#tos)

TOS


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Discord TOSarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/terms)
    
*   [Twitch TOSarrow-up-right](https://www.twitch.tv/p/en/legal/terms-of-service/??utm_referrer=https://www.google.com/)
    
*   [Kick TOSarrow-up-right](https://kick.com/terms-of-service)
    

SSRP is a streamer friendly server, to maintain a healthy environment. all players must follow the general streaming Terms of Services provided by _**Twitch, Kick, TikTok, & Youtube**_. This means any content streamed or uploaded from SSRP must follow TOS, which includes and not limited to hate speech, harassments in all forms, and unsuitable content. This ensures our community is a welcoming environment to those who are making content, and those who are just trying to enjoy our server.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#microphone-requirement)

**Microphone Requirement**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All players must have a functioning microphone to be able to play the server to ensure smooth, and engaging experiences. However, if you can't use a microphone for personal reasons like illnesses, or disabilities, please speak to a server administrator as soon as possible so it is communicated to the staff team to prevent further issues.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#gameplay-addons)

Gameplay - Addons


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Use of Sound & Graphics Packs** The use of custom sound packs, graphic mods, and other visual enhancement packs are permitted on the server provided they do not offer any gameplay or tactical advantage or alter core game mechanics (such as props or map assets).

*   Prohibited modifications include, but are not limited to:
    
*   Amplified or unusually loud footsteps
    
*   Removal or alteration of props/objects
    
*   Visual filters or effects that improve visibility beyond intended game limits
    

**Only standard day/night visual packs are allowed.** **Immersion Enhancements Only:**

*   All packs should be used strictly to improve immersion or realism, not to gain an advantage over other players.
    
*   **Day & Night cycle Graphics packs**
    
    *   Night has to be dark
        
    *   All props & vegetation has to be included
        
    *   Pack has to be on the realistic side
        
    
*   **Regular thin tracers are allowed**
    
    *   No slow tracers
        
    *   No big / thick tracers
        
    
*   **Custom weapon sound packs are allowed**
    
    *   No loud footsteps
        
    *   Headshot SFX are acceptable
        
        *   Has to be on the realistic side ( example: no coin headshot SFX )
            
        *   Example of allowed ( Headshot Crunch )
            
        
    
*   **Regular Kill effects are allowed**
    
    *   No Xray kill effects
        
    *   Has to be realistic
        
    
*   **Blood Effects are Allowed**
    
    *   Has to be on the realistic side
        
    *   No unrealistic effects
        
    
*   **ALL** and any advantage RPF files or any other sort of unfair advantage modifications are not allowed & considered exploiting.
    
*   Everything that is allowed has to be some what realistic or roleplay acceptable
    

**Example:** Improved weapon sounds or lighting adjustments that maintain normal visibility are acceptable.

**Staff Discretion**

*   Server staff reserve the right to require the removal of any sound or graphics pack that is determined to provide an unfair roleplay or gameplay advantage.
    

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#gameplay-recording)

**Gameplay Recording**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For gang and cheating reports, players are required to use AMD or NVIDIA clipping software only. No other recording or clipping software will be accepted for these report types.

For regular player reports, such as RDM or TOS violations, any clipping software may be used, including Medal.

If a player is found using unapproved software for gang or cheating reports, they will be issued a “Must Stream” role and will be required to use approved clipping software for all gameplay sessions. For more information regarding gameplay recording requirements, please refer to the Player Reports Policy.

SSRP is here to create a polite and safe environment for everyone involved. Toxic behaviors and fostering toxicity in any way will not be tolerated. This includes, but is not limited to, harassment, sexual harassment, hate speech, racism, personal remarks, etc. We expect all members to contribute to a friendly environment, and breaching this policy may result in permanent removal from our community. This includes to doxing, exposing or spreading information about our community members.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#rule-misuse-of-chat-commands)

**Rule:** Misuse of Chat Commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The misuse of any chat command that displays messages in the top-left corner of the screen (including but not limited to /ooclocal, /me, /shout, /say, or similar) is **strictly prohibited**. These commands must only be used for their intended roleplay purposes.

*   Spamming or flooding chat
    
*   Using OOC commands to disrupt active roleplay
    
*   Trolling other players
    
*   **Using commands to bypass proximity or gain unfair advantages**
    
*   Posting out-of-character (OOC) information in in-character (IC) chats
    
*   Excessive capitalization or non-roleplay text that breaks immersion
    

All chat commands should be used respectfully and in a way that maintains roleplay quality and server immersion. **Failure to follow this rule may result in disciplinary action based off your infraction history**

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#real-money-trading)

**Real Money Trading**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You are prohibited from selling in-game items for out of city money. Doing so will result in a permanent ban to all parties involved.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#no-staff-impersonation)

**No Staff Impersonation**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Staff impersonation isn't tolerated, and doing so may result in disciplinary actions.

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge#server-events)

Server Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Public ( Staff Managed) Server events are Green Zones. You cannot build interactions during events. (Parties club events and business events ARE greenzones).

[PreviousCharacter Creationchevron-left](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/getting-started/character-creation)
[NextPlayer Reports Policychevron-right](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/rules/general_knowledge/player-reports-policy)

# SSRP EMS | Southside | Wiki

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252F2GzsAPVjwIkJ1RVgLplY%252FSS_EMS.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd9104a8-ba43-41b7-9e9c-390611be9e84&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d8dfee5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/recruitment/ssrp-ems#requirements-to-join-ssrp-ems)

**Requirements to Join SSRP EMS:**

*   You must be **truthful** about your age. You must be 18+ to apply.
    
*   **Everyone** should be reading the SOP **before** beginning their experience.,
    
*   There will be a weekly hour requirement of **10 hours minimum**. Any complications with fulfilling them should be **communicated** to a higher up.,
    
*   Everyone must undergo **basic training** with a higher up. You will be taught everything you need to know including procedures and rules.,
    
*   **Server/In-City** rules **MUST** be followed at **ALL** times. If you are caught violating any rules you will be at risk of being **stripped** and/or **banned**.,
    
*   All recruits must **pair up** for a ride-along throughout the recruitment process unless **otherwise promoted** and given the okay.

# SSRP DOJ | Southside | Wiki

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252FrIJIPc431Hlxky1p2o5C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7598c1ce-dbf8-4828-b7f5-165bec7cd062&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7175d91&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/recruitment/ssrp-doj#requirements-to-join-the-doj)

**Requirements to Join the DOJ:**

• You must be 18 years or older and truthful about your age. • You must thoroughly read and understand the DOJ SOP and server rules before beginning your role. • A minimum weekly activity requirement must be maintained (court sessions, case work, meetings, or filings). Failure to meet activity expectations without communication may result in removal. • You must complete a mandatory training and evaluation period under DOJ leadership before full promotion. • Professionalism is required at all times — both in-character and out-of-character. • You must demonstrate the ability to remain unbiased and ethical, even in high-pressure or high-profile cases. • All DOJ members are expected to prioritize story-driven RP over “winning” cases. • Proper documentation, filings, and case preparation are required — low-effort work will not be accepted. • Confidential information must remain strictly within DOJ channels. • You may not hold positions that create a conflict of interest (subject to leadership review). • Inactivity without notice may result in demotion or removal. • DOJ leadership reserves the right to remove members who fail to uphold department standards.

* * *

**. To apply click** [**here**arrow-up-right](https://dashboard.southsiderp.net/applications/doj)
**.**

# SSRP Real Estate | Southside | Wiki

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252F5nuJBpFkicVNRAb1qKEq%252FSS_RE.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc94c365b-5a49-4463-9dac-7a43a6b81549&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4be02da2&sv=2)

*   **Please** use the discords application process to apply to be a part of the team.,
    
*   SSRP is a 18+ server and you will be required as a staff member to inform us so you can have the proper roles,
    
*   Read over ALL of the rules both for the discord and also for your position in the city,
    
*   Everyone will receive a standard position in the beginning and with time you will level up in the ranks,
    
*   You will be required to log everything you do with a property,
    
*   NO discounts for friends or family at any point, if caught you will be stripped and won’t have a chance to be a part of the team again,
    
*   Unannounced LOA’S or excessive amounts of your absence will result in the removal of your position.
    

* * *

Click here to join the [**discord**arrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/sK7DGU5YeA)
**. To apply click** [**here**arrow-up-right](https://dashboard.southsiderp.net/applications/realestate)
**.**

# SSRP Police Department | Southside | Wiki

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252Frbf7aCtjQHTeSP06qCJj%252FSS_PD.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D572a6960-07a1-41ff-963d-7d5853873a5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46ec84d9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/recruitment/ssrp-police-department#requirements-to-join-the-ssrp-pd)

Requirements to Join the SSRP PD:

*   We request all officers to be 18+
    
*   All officers will need to do a Interview within there first week of being hired on.
    
*   All officers main language must be English
    
*   Will be given SOPs before being hired and will be expected to know them by first week
    
*   Will be expected to put 7 hours of on duty time per week unless LOA is in
    
*   Willing to learn and work with others
    
*   Go through a one week period of being a Cadet and trained by a FTO (could take longer)
    
*   PD MUST be recording (Body Cam) at all times
    
*   In Person interviews are a must to be hired
    

* * *

**Click here to join the** [**discord**arrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/ZSVYNYMgjb)
**. To apply click** [**here**arrow-up-right](https://dashboard.southsiderp.net/applications/police)
**.**

# Introduction | Southside | Wiki

![](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3417382440-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FDGUwqbfsl8y8e1Sy9KYg%252Fuploads%252Fp6CbH5XEE7RzmZrZr83U%252FSouthside%2520Reality%2520Map.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43e4d677-8ccd-4b04-9915-d4fec69fae71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7c92813&sv=2)

If you have questions, please go to the discord and to the respective channels.

### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#property-tier-pricing-by-district)

🏘️ Property Tier Pricing by District

Below is a breakdown of property pricing tiers by district. All prices are subject to change with the city’s economy.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#red-district)

🔴 Red District

*   **Tier 1:** $200,000 – $300,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $350,000 – $450,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $500,000+
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#industrial-zone)

*   **Tier 1:** $50,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $75,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $150,000+
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#downtown)

🪩 Downtown

*   **Tier 1:** $350,000 – $450,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $500,000 – $600,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $700,000 – $800,000+
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#east-beach)

🌊 East Beach

*   **Tier 1:** $50,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $75,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $125,000+
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#glen-park)

🌲 Glen Park

*   **Tier 1:** $350,000 – $400,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $450,000 – $500,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $550,000 – $1,500,000+
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://wiki.southsiderp.net/housing/introduction#west-beach)

🌴West Beach

*   **Tier 1:** $700,000 – $750,000
    
*   **Tier 2:** $800,000 – $1,000,000
    
*   **Tier 3:** $1,000,000 – $2,000,000+
